        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer181230913" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6367012586118857342">Also found here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://christianbookshelfreviews.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-maid-at-fairbourne-hall-by-julie.html'>http://christianbookshelfreviews.blog...</a><br/><br/><br/>Before I share what I thought about The Maid of Fairbourne Hall, I have to mention that Julie Klassen is one of my mom's favorite authors - she's read all of Julie's books and when she saw that I had this book for review - she immediately took it from me and had to read it first! And guess what? My mom loved this book from the first sentence on... literally!<br/><br/>While Julie Klassen is not a new author to my mom, she is to me - this is the first</span>
  <span id="freeText6367012586118857342" style="display:none">Also found here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://christianbookshelfreviews.blogspot.com/2012/01/review-maid-at-fairbourne-hall-by-julie.html">http://christianbookshelfreviews.blog...</a><br /><br /><br />Before I share what I thought about The Maid of Fairbourne Hall, I have to mention that Julie Klassen is one of my mom's favorite authors - she's read all of Julie's books and when she saw that I had this book for review - she immediately took it from me and had to read it first! And guess what? My mom loved this book from the first sentence on... literally!<br /><br />While Julie Klassen is not a new author to my mom, she is to me - this is the first book I've read of hers and I don't know why. It was phenomenal! Absolutely stunning and vivid in details! If all of her other books are like this one, I've completely been missing out.<br /><br /><b>"He is reading my letters now too...."</b><br /><br />That opening sentence had me wondering who was reading her letters? What else had this person been doing? There is so much just in that first sentence! :)<br /><br />The characters in The Maid of Fairbourne Hall had such interesting stories and what happened between Margaret and Nathaniel years ago made it impossible for me not to care for these characters and what would happen in their lives.<br /><br />This is shocking to me, since this book is over 400 pages long, but I read The Maid of Fairbourne Hall in less than 24 hours! I couldn't stop reading for long, and after a few pages/chapters, I was hooked. It was that good and entertaining that I found there wasn't a good place to stop and before I knew it I was done with the book! Too soon, I might add - I was not ready to say goodbye to the characters. I'm hoping for a sequel (as I normally do with books I love).<br /><br />My mom and I don't always agree about books, but in this case we do. The Maid of Fairbourne Hall by Julie Klassen is a definite winner and as you can see from the award above, this is now a favorite book of mine! I 100%, without a doubt, recommend this book - especially if you enjoy reading historical novels!! <br /><br />*I received a complimentary copy of this book from the publisher via CFBA. I was not required to give a positive review, only my honest opinion - which I've done. All thoughts and opinions are my own.*</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ummu Auni" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ummu Auni" href="/user/show/1091055-ummu-auni">Ummu Auni</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1091055-ummu-auni?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1091055-ummu-auni?shelf=clean-romance">clean-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1091055-ummu-auni?shelf=read-2013">read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1091055-ummu-auni?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer647141674" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2150737056692286530">I enjoyed reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12820360.Edenbrooke' title='Edenbrooke by Julianne Donaldson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Edenbrooke</a> so much that I felt I should give a try for other romance that falls under this genre. I picked this one up after searching 'clean romance' tag. This is the first book that I read from this author.<br/><br/>Maid of Fairbourne Hall outlined the story of Margaret who ran away from home to escape his step father's arrangement ended up being a maid at one of the places that she thought she wouldn't be - Fairbourne Hall. There resides her former suitor, Nathaniel. Margaret used to </span>
  <span id="freeText2150737056692286530" style="display:none">I enjoyed reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12820360.Edenbrooke" title="Edenbrooke by Julianne Donaldson" rel="nofollow noopener">Edenbrooke</a> so much that I felt I should give a try for other romance that falls under this genre. I picked this one up after searching 'clean romance' tag. This is the first book that I read from this author.<br /><br />Maid of Fairbourne Hall outlined the story of Margaret who ran away from home to escape his step father's arrangement ended up being a maid at one of the places that she thought she wouldn't be - Fairbourne Hall. There resides her former suitor, Nathaniel. Margaret used to reject him in the hope of winning his handsome brother's heart - a flirt, a heart breaker.<br /><br />The plot is predictable, but what I enjoyed most is the detailing on the lives of the household's servants. Reading this, I can actually craft a surrounding among the servants. There are two levels of servants, the upper level and the lower level. Having a keen interest on Downton Abbey certainly helped.<br /><br />There are some things too good to be true, on how Margaret, a gentle lady, under a disguise of being a maid was able to cope with the tasks given, but ah yes, this is much more made on surreal things. What I enjoyed most is the fact the habits and the routines of the servants. It's interesting to read that kind of view especially when the author did research on this.<br /><br />Nathaniel, the hero is someone that I assume, maybe in the first place, looks common, but then, he was able to stand out among others. I found myself pining for him. The conflict of Nathan with his siblings, and then, his stand on slavery, made it much more welcoming. The author also injected an element of surprise especially on Nathaniel's brother's injuries. <br /><br />Few sweet elements include the Monsieur Fournier, sweet admiration to Mrs. Budgeon, the housekeeper. And the wonderfully written ending when Margaret thought she lost Nathaniel.<br /><br />Since this is the first novel I read, I tend to be bias though. a 3.5 star or maybe a-4. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2150737056692286530" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_212901970" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/212901970" />
    <a title="eve v." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6018037-eve-v"><img alt="eve v." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563237009p2/6018037.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/212901970?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="eve v." class="user" itemprop="url" name="eve v." href="/user/show/6018037-eve-v">eve v.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6018037-eve-v?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6018037-eve-v?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6018037-eve-v?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer212901970" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16838031306696655211">This is it. I am SO going to buy every Julie Klassen book there is this year! It's officially on my 2012 to-do list.<br/>Where do I even start?! This book was beyond amazing... it was amazingly amazing, amazing! The whole lady-in-disguise thing was really intriguing, to me at least - I'm a lover of disguises! ;D<br/>Margaret (or should I say Nora? ;) was a very strong female character. I mean, running away from home, to escape from the greedy hands of a stepfather and his puppet nephew, to go work as a ma</span>
  <span id="freeText16838031306696655211" style="display:none">This is it. I am SO going to buy every Julie Klassen book there is this year! It's officially on my 2012 to-do list.<br />Where do I even start?! This book was beyond amazing... it was amazingly amazing, amazing! The whole lady-in-disguise thing was really intriguing, to me at least - I'm a lover of disguises! ;D<br />Margaret (or should I say Nora? ;) was a very strong female character. I mean, running away from home, to escape from the greedy hands of a stepfather and his puppet nephew, to go work as a maid somewhere? That would take lots of courage. And the fact that the 'somewhere' turned out to be Fairbourne Hall, the home of two of Margaret's former suitors, farther complicated things.<br />Nathaniel was the PERFECT match for Margaret. A God-fearing, protective, handsome gentleman... what more could you want?! ;P<br />Lewis, or ummm... Lewie, was oh so very spoiled. From the first few chapters I was convinced he was one of those 'gentlemen' you certainly don't want to get too close to... unless, of course, you intend to bang him on the head with something (like I don't know... maybe a <a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/60869032433379704/" rel="nofollow noopener">frying pan</a>? ;D).<br />I loved the ending as well. It was so sweet! &lt;3 Julie Klassen has this amazing ability to end a book with just enough detail, as to satisfy, yet not too much, as to give your imagination something to work on (like plan a wedding, for example ;).<br />The only thing I was kind of disappointed about though, was that Margaret didn't get to reveal herself to the servants of Fairbourne Hall. I would've loved to find out their reactions... especially Betty's and Fiona's!<br />Anyways, if you haven't already, go read this book... RIGHT NOW!!! You won't be disappointed! :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16838031306696655211" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('i7d9AN4GBESbDqCiBa8fdVKgCSifuAUPTZmV4mbyNQ0kWKeMFfhD/Iw+Q9mTGsTAXb8M4W8jJahXZCysvEYTTQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kRWJhXCNcLmjVjc2lJXckYKrQfVie+32EP0w3ioBqcU++lMJu3M3AbRm1E0CIAckjbREPJLgzVEKAImQ8LWPhQ==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/928415.Julie_Klassen">About Julie Klassen</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/928415.Julie_Klassen"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1438099690p3/928415.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/928415.Julie_Klassen">Julie Klassen

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14244257520992093410">Julie Klassen loves all things Jane—<i>Jane Eyre</i> and Jane Austen. A graduate of the University of Illinois, Julie worked in publishing for sixteen years and now writes full time. Three of her books, <i>The Silent Governess</i>, <i>The Girl in the Gatehouse</i>, and <i>The Maid of Fairbourne Hall</i>, have won the Christy Award for Historical Romance. She has also won the Midwest Book Award, the Minnesota Book Award, and </span>
  <span id="freeText14244257520992093410" style="display:none">Julie Klassen loves all things Jane—<i>Jane Eyre</i> and Jane Austen. A graduate of the University of Illinois, Julie worked in publishing for sixteen years and now writes full time. Three of her books, <i>The Silent Governess</i>, <i>The Girl in the Gatehouse</i>, and <i>The Maid of Fairbourne Hall</i>, have won the Christy Award for Historical Romance. She has also won the Midwest Book Award, the Minnesota Book Award, and Christian Retailing’s BEST Award, and been a finalist in the Romance Writers of America’s RITA Awards and ACFW’s Carol Awards. She blogs at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.inspiredbylifeandfiction.com">http://www.inspiredbylifeandfiction.com</a>.<br />Julie and her husband have two sons and live in a suburb of St. Paul, Minnesota. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14244257520992093410" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

Then she smiled at him, her eyes brimming with tears. “Yes, it most definitely has.&rdquo;</span>
